# Web Language : Living


This is the dataset for Living languages.

This language list is generated from ISO-639-3, with some additions.
If your favorite language is missing, please open an issue on Github.



## Languages with more than 50mm speakers

- [Amharic](amharic.md)
- Arabic: See Modern Standard Arabic, and many others
- [Bengali](bengali.md)
- [Bhojpuri](bhojpuri.md)
- Chinese: See Mandarin Chinese and the many other Chinese languages
- [Egyptian Arabic](egyptian_arabic.md)
- English
- French
- German
- [Gujarati](gujarati.md)
- [Hausa](hausa.md)
- [Hindi](hindi.md)
- [Indonesian](indonesian.md)
- [Iranian Persian](iranian_persian.md)
- [Italian](italian.md)
- [Japanese](japanese.md)
- [Javanese](javanese.md)
- [Kannada](kannada.md)
- [Korean](korean.md)
- Lahnda: See Western Panjabi and many others
- [Levantine Arabic](levantine_arabic.md)
- Malay (macrolanguage): See Indonesian, and 34 other languages with Malay in their name
- [Mandarin Chinese](mandarin_chinese.md)
- [Marathi](marathi.md)
- [Min Nan Chinese](min_nan_chinese.md)
- [Nigerian Pidgin](nigerian_pidgin.md)
- Persian: See Iranian Persian, Dari, and Tajik
- [Portuguese](portuguese.md) Includes Brazil, we may break that out later
- Russian
- Spanish: We may eventually make a geographic breakdown
- [Standard Arabic](standard_arabic.md)
- [Swahili (individual language)](swahili_individual_language_.md)
- [Tagalog](tagalog.md)
- [Tamil](tamil.md)
- [Telugu](telugu.md)
- [Thai](thai.md)
- [Turkish](turkish.md)
- [Urdu](urdu.md)
- [Vietnamese](vietnamese.md)
- [Western Panjabi](western_panjabi.md)
- [Wu Chinese](wu_chinese.md)
- [Yue Chinese](yue_chinese.md)
